### NSLOCTEXT
```angelscript
FText NSLOCTEXT(FString Namespace, FString Key, FString Text)
```
Function for using localization texts in Angelscript. Emulates NSLOCTEXT macro.
Only string literals can be used as input arguments from Angelscript.
Using variables (like FString) will run but will cause errors when strings are gathered for localization.
